# Module Card: run-stage-categorize-enrich

Owner: pipeline-flow-owner

## Purpose

Assign categories, persist category drafts, and enrich attributes with first/second pass logic.

## When To Use

After ingest/sampling and before embedding/persistence stages.

## Inputs

Sampled normalized products, providers, config thresholds, logger, stage timing map.

## Outputs

Category assignments, persisted categories map, taxonomy metadata, enrichment map, enrichment stats.

## Steps

1. Run category assignment for sampled products.\n2. Build and persist category drafts.\n3. Execute attribute enrichment batches.\n4. Optionally run selective second-pass enrichment.\n5. Return enrichment outputs and counters.

## Failure Signals

Category persistence mismatch, enrichment batch failures, excessive fallback enrichment rates.

## Related Files

- 
- 

## Related Commands

- 
> experiments-w-rob@0.1.0 pipeline
> tsx src/cli/pipeline.ts\n- 
> experiments-w-rob@0.1.0 canary
> tsx src/cli/canary-run.ts
